ba_in01,375,102,0	script	#ep19evt01	HIDDEN_WARP_NPC,3,3,{
	end;
OnTouch:
	if (ep19_main == 1) {
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19elly01" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19lazy01" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19crux01" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19miriam02" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19maram02" );
		end;
	}
	if (ep19_main == 2) {
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19elly01" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19lazy01" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19crux01" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19miriam02" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19maram02" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19gg02" );
		end;
	}
	end;
}

	end;
OnTouch:
	if (ep19_main == 34) {
		if (isbegin_quest(16636) == 1) {
			unittalk getcharid(3), "" + strcharinfo(0) + " : เข้าไปลึกกว่านี้กันเถอะ", bc_self;
			setquest 16639;
			setquest 16640;
			erasequest 16636;
		}
		if (isbegin_quest(16639) == 1)
			cloakoffnpcself( "ep19_ep19re1_C" );
		if (isbegin_quest(16640) == 1)
			cloakoffnpcself( "ep19_ep19re2_C" );
		end;
	}
	if (ep19_main == 36) {
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19_jor_nest_31_140" );
		end;
	}
	if (ep19_main >= 38 && ep19_main <= 42) {
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19_jor_nest_31_140" );
		end;
	}
	if (ep19_main == 45) {	// Step 53
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19_jor_nest_19_190" );
		end;
	}
	if (ep19_main == 46 || ep19_main == 47) {	// Step 54, 55
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19_jor_nest_19_190" );
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19_jor_nest_20_194" );
		end;
	}
	if (ep19_main == 48) {	// Step 56
		cloakoffnpcself( "ep19_jor_nest_24_185" );
		end;
	}
	end;
}

	mes "ยังไม่มีความเคลื่อนไหวที่น่าสงสัย";
	close;

	end;

	questinfo( QTYPE_QUEST2, QMARK_YELLOW, "isbegin_quest(17644) == 1" );
	end;
